# Meta data

<pre>
Ramon benchmark for Z3
-
Job description: QF_NIA_small, explain_fixed_column_no_join branch, default options, seed 1
Job tag: explain_fixed_column_no_join_vs_master_qfnia_small_20_rs_1
Runner: rise-runner-2
Z3 repo: Z3Prover/z3
Z3 commit: 6aef4aaab79431f1e2c8db59991c6804123d7f19
Z3 branch: explain_fixed_column_no_join
Z3 options: "-T:20 smt.random_seed=1"
Z3 inputs: inputs/QF_NIA_small
Z3 commit message: lp: avoid mk_join allocation in explain_fixed_column

explain_fixed_column is invoked once per fixed column per row from
explain_fixed_in_row and showed up as 25.5% self time, dominated by the
per-call mk_join allocation that builds a throw-away join node only to
immediately flatten it (and those nodes accumulate in the dependency
allocator for the lifetime of the solve).

Linearize the lower and upper bound witnesses directly via a new
flatten(a, b) overload that pushes the (at most two) non-null witnesses
into a single linearize pass, eliminating the allocation entirely while
preserving dedup semantics.

Co-authored-by: Copilot <223556219+Copilot@users.noreply.github.com>

</pre>
